in Portuguese, English and Spanish, this simulator provides the possibility to investigate the Projectile Movement in a 3D perspective.\r\nThe study of the movement of projectiles is very important because it allows the approach of movement in two dimensions. In this movement, the projectiles are launched and subjected to a downward  constant acceleration due to the force of gravity, causing the projectiles to describe a parabolic trajectory. Within the study of projectile motion, the determination of the range and its relation with the angle of launch are also very important.\r\nSeeking to approach the concepts contained in the projectile movement, this simulator brings two scenarios, each one with different gravity values: the Earth and the Moon. In both of them, there is a cannon that fires projectiles across the scenario. In the Earth there is a wall with some dynamites to be hit and cylinder collectors to approach the concept of horizontal range. This also motivates the child to want to get higher awards and better marks.\r\n\r\nThere are 39 subtopics categorized as follows:\r\n\r\nNumbers\r\n\r\n1.\tWrite\r\n2.\tCounting in Powers of 10\r\n3.\tPlace Value\r\n4.\tRounding\r\n5.\tCompare\r\n6.\tPrime\r\n7.\tSquare and Cube\r\n8.\tRoman Numerals\r\n\r\nCalculations\r\n\r\n9.\tAddition\r\n10.\tSubtraction\r\n11.\tMultiplication\r\n12.\tDivision\r\n13.\tEstimating\r\n14.\tSolve Problems\r\n\r\nFractions\r\n\r\n15.\t Simplify\r\n16.\tAddition\r\n17.\tSubtraction\r\n18.\tMultiplication\r\n19.\tConvert\r\n20.\tSolve Problems\r\n\r\nDecimals\r\n\r\n21.\t Addition\r\n22.\t Subtraction\r\n23.\tDividing by 10 or 100\r\n24.\t Place Value\r\n25.\t Rounding\r\n26.\t Compare\r\n27.\tConvert\r\n28.\t Solve Problems\r\n\r\nMeasurements\r\n\r\n29.\t Length Mass and Volume\r\n30.\t Area and Perimeter \r\n31.\tEstimating Volume\r\n32.\t Time\r\n33.\t Money\r\n34.\t Solve Problems\r\n\r\nGeometry\r\n\r\n35.\t Angles\r\n36.\tNets\r\n37.\t Coordinates\r\n38.\t Reflection\r\n\r\nStatistics\r\n\r\n39.\tCharts\r\n\r\nTEST RESULTS\r\nOn the completion of each test the user is given a summary of questions answered correctly and incorrectly, the percentage achieved in the test and the time taken on each test. This has been invaluable for top performing children who have achieved diamond status as they can improve on the time the tests are taking them.
